<script type="text/javascript"> // <![CDATA[

window.ptaHpFadeHeadline = 1;

window.isSafari = /constructor/i.test(window.HTMLElement) || (function (p) { return p.toString() === "[object SafariRemoteNotification]"; })(!window['safari'] || safari.pushNotification) || !!(window.navigator.userAgent.match('AppleWebKit') && !window.navigator.userAgent.match('Chrome'));
window.newVisitor = document.cookie.indexOf(analyticsdatalayer.sessionid + 'UAL') === -1;

(function() {

    function _renderHeadline() {
        var svg = document.querySelector('svg.headline'),
            tspans = svg.querySelectorAll('tspan'),
            textNodes = svg.querySelectorAll('text'),
            tspans = svg.getElementsByTagName("tspan"),
            textNodes = svg.getElementsByTagName("text"),
            maxWidth = 0,
            maxHeight = 0,
            idx = 0;

        // fix sub/sup tag positioning (can't use baseline-adjust because of IE)
        for (idx = 0; idx < tspans.length; idx++) {
          var tspan = tspans[idx],
          classList = tspan.getAttribute("class").toLowerCase();
          if ((tspan.classlist && tspan.classList.contains("sup")) || classList === "sup") {
            tspan.setAttribute("dy", "-30px");
            } else if ((tspan.classlist && tspan.classList.contains("sub")) || classList === "sub") {
              tspan.setAttribute("dy", "30px");
            }
          }

          for (idx=0; idx < textNodes.length; idx++) {
            var textNode = textNodes[idx],
            bb = textNode.getBBox(),
            width = Math.ceil(bb.width),
            height = Math.ceil(bb.height);

            textNode.setAttribute("textLength", width);
            maxWidth = Math.max(maxWidth, width);
            maxHeight = Math.max(maxHeight, height);
          }

          svg.setAttribute("viewBox", "0 0 " + (maxWidth+24) + " " + (maxHeight+24));
          Array.prototype.forEach.call(textNodes, function (node) {
            if (node.classList) {

                if (isSafari && newVisitor && (ptaHpFadeHeadline === 1)) {
                    node.classList.remove('initial');
                    node.classList.add('fadeIn');
                } else {
                    node.classList.remove('fade');
                    node.classList.remove('initial');
                }

            } else {
                node.className = 'rendered';
                node.style.visibility = 'visible';
            }
          })
    }

    if (isSafari && newVisitor && (ptaHpFadeHeadline === 1)) {
        window.addEventListener("load", function() {
            _renderHeadline();
        });
    } else {
        _renderHeadline();
    }

})();
